CREATE TABLE TB_PATIENT_INFO (
   pnt_uid VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
   pnt_name NVARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   resi_no VARCHAR(7) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   birth_date DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   birth_division CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   hp_no VARCHAR(16) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   home_tel VARCHAR(16) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   email NVARCHAR(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   work_image_id INT NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   home_zipcd VARCHAR(6) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   home_addr NVARCHAR(100) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   home_addr2 NVARCHAR(100) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   registration_date DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   lastvisit_date DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   doctor_uid VARCHAR(20) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   hygienist VARCHAR(20) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   sms_recv_yn CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   personal_info_yn CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   email_recv_yn CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   hipaa_assent_yn CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   work_graphic_id INT NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   protector_hp VARCHAR(16) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   protector_sms_yn CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   family_id VARCHAR(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   patient_relation_id INT NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   visit_id VARCHAR(100) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   pnt_int NUMERIC(20,0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   rrn VARCHAR(24) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   day_seq NUMERIC(18,0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   del_yn CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT 'N',
   pnt_nickname VARCHAR(8) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
   PRIMARY KEY (pnt_uid)
)
;

ALTER TABLE "TB_PATIENT_INFO" ALTER COLUMN "pnt_int" NUMERIC(20,8)
ALTER TABLE "TB_PATIENT_INFO" ALTER COLUMN "day_seq" NUMERIC(18,8)
